                  <foreign lang="ar">مُزَارَعَةٌ</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">the making a contract,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">bargain, with another to cultivate land for a share of its produce</hi>], (AO, Lh, S, A, IAth, Mgh, Msb,) <hi rend="ital">for somewhat of its produce,</hi> (S, Msb,) or <hi rend="ital">for a third</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a quarter,</hi> (AO, Mgh,) or <hi rend="ital">for a determined share, such as a third or a quarter</hi> or <hi rend="ital">some other portion,</hi> (IAth,) or <hi rend="ital">for half</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like:</hi> (so in some copies of the K and in the TA:) or the <hi rend="ital">tilling the ground for half</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like:</hi> (so in other copies of the K:) and <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مُؤَاكَرَةٌ</foreign>: (K:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9886-2-1" target="خِبْرٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n9891"/></foreign> is syn. with <foreign lang="ar">مُخَابَرَةٌ</foreign>: (S, K:) it is a forbidden practice: (A, Mgh, TA:) it is from <foreign lang="ar">خَبِيرٌ</foreign> signifying “ a tiller, or cultivator, of land: ” (S, Mgh:) or from <foreign lang="ar">خَبَرَ</foreign> “ he furrowed, or ploughed (land) for sowing; ” whence <foreign lang="ar">خَبِيرٌ</foreign> also: (Msb:) or from <foreign lang="ar">خَبِرَتِ الأَرْضُ</foreign> “ the land abounded with <foreign lang="ar">خَبَار</foreign>: ” or from [the fortress of] <foreign lang="ar">خَيْبَر</foreign>, because the Prophet made it to remain in the possession of its inhabitants for half of its revenue; and therefore it was said, <foreign lang="ar">خَابَرَهُمْ</foreign>.                   <foreign lang="ar">جِرْذَان</foreign> [or <hi rend="ital">large field-rats</hi>]: (K:) [a coll. gen. n.:] n. un. with <foreign lang="ar">ة</foreign>. (TA.)    </entryFree>2f:T1112,<entryFree id="n9899" key="خَبِيرٌ" type="main">

                  <hi rend="ital">Knowing; having knowledge;</hi> (S, A, Msb;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9899-1" target="خَبِرٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n9893"/></foreign>: (AHn:) or <hi rend="ital">possessing much knowledge with respect to internal things;</hi> like <foreign lang="ar">شَهِيدٌ</foreign> with respect to external things: (L in art. <foreign lang="ar">شهد</foreign>:) or <hi rend="ital">possessing knowledge of matters of information, news, tidings, accounts, narratives, or stories; of what is termed</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">خَبَرٌ</foreign>; (K;) or <hi rend="ital">of what are termed</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَخْبَار</foreign>; (TA;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9899-2" target="خَابِرٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n9902"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9899-3" target="خَبِرٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n9893"/></foreign>, (K,) which last is thought by ISd to be a possessive [as distinguished from a verbal] epithet, (TA,) [or it is from <foreign lang="ar">خَبِرَ</foreign>, a form which ISd may not have known,] and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9899-4" target="خُبْرٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n9890"/></foreign>, (K,) which is an intensive epithet: (TA:) also <hi rend="ital">informed; possessing information.</hi> (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">أَنَا بِهِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">خَبِيرٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I have knowledge of it.</hi> (A.) And [hence] <foreign lang="ar">الخَبِيرُ</foreign> is a name of God, meaning <hi rend="ital">He who knoweth what hath been and what is or will be:</hi> (TA:) or <hi rend="ital">He who well knoweth the internal qualities of things.</hi> (Sharh Et-Tirmidhee.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">Possessing knowledge of God,</hi> (K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">by being acquainted with his names and his attributes.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A lawyer; one skilled in the law,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">practical religion.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A head,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">chief.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A tiller,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">cultivator, of land.</hi> (S, Mgh, Msb, K.)       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">Fur,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">soft hair,</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">وَبَرٌ</foreign>, (S, K,) of camels, and <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  of the wild ass. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">Hair that has fallen:</hi> and with <foreign lang="ar">ة</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">a portion thereof.</hi> (K.)
